| S-001 | security | Returns raw `(e as Error).message` (network/socket error text) to the client. | S-004 | security | GET returns `error: \`Steam sync failed: ${safe}\`` containing the raw masked error message. | S-006 | security | `saveProxyConfig` does **not** type-check `patch.username` or `patch.password` before reading them. `(patch.username as string) ?? A malicious settings PATCH can store a 1 MB string. | `src/lib/proxy-config.ts:220-228` | — | Loopback-gated. DoS-via-storage. Also serialised back through `JSON.stringify` and stored in `app_setting`, where the row size is unbounded. | TODO |

| S-031 | security | Unauthed image-proxy GET. Validates IDs, fetches via SSRF-allowlisted hops, but each call may issue 1-4 outbound fetches. A LAN attacker can hammer it to push outbound bandwidth. | `src/app/api/egs-cover/[id]/route.ts:259-307` | — | DoS amplification. | TODO |

| S-033 | security | No auth gate; the storage root contains user-uploaded covers/banners (no PII per se, but unique-content). Path-traversal is blocked (line 17). Mime-type forced to octet-stream for SVG. | `src/app/api/files/[...path]/route.ts:14-22` | — | Information disclosure: anyone on the LAN can enumerate stored files when they know a path. | TODO |
| S-034 | security | Path-traversal guard is `rel.includes('..')` — also catches benign filenames like `foo..bar.jpg`. The `readStored` helper does proper normalisation, so this is defence-in-depth, but the check rejects more than necessary. Stronger / more precise: use `normalize` and compare against `STORAGE_ROOT`. | `src/app/api/files/[...path]/route.ts:17` | — | Functional false positive (no security issue). | TODO |
| S-035 | security | EGS SQL is constructed with template-string interpolation: `WHERE g.id = ${id}`, `WHERE game = ${gameId}`, `LIMIT ${safeLimit}`. The numeric values come from `Number(...)` + `Number.isInteger` upstream and `safeLimit` is clamped. Strings flow through `sanitizeForEgsLike`. So no concrete injection today, but the practice is fragile. | `src/lib/erogamescape.ts:411, 474, 813` | — | Future regression risk — if a new caller passes an unvalidated numeric, EGS's remote Postgres will execute it. | TODO |
| S-036 | security | `code` URL segment is **not validated** against the `^\d{3}-\d{6}-\d{3}$` shape expected by the rest of the kobe pipeline. Calls `getKobeStockItem(code)` (returns null for unknown), `setKobeVnLink(code, ...)` (UPDATE no-ops), `clearKobeVnLink(code)` (UPDATE no-ops). Parameterised so no SQLi, but `recordActivity` (line 23) stores the unvalidated `code` as `entityId` and `label`. | `src/app/api/alicesoft-kobe/[code]/link/route.ts:11-25` | — | A malicious POST writes attacker-controlled payload into `user_activity.entity_id` and `user_activity.label`. Loopback-gated; defence-in-depth. | TODO |
| S-037 | security | `body.params` is accepted as `typeof === 'string'` but never length-capped. The saved-filter URL fragment is stored verbatim in `saved_filter.params`. | `src/app/api/saved-filters/route.ts:18-32` | — | Loopback-gated; DoS via huge string. | TODO |
| S-038 | security | `body.logged_at` accepted as any positive number — including `Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER`. Inserted as `INTEGER` epoch. | `src/app/api/collection/[id]/game-log/route.ts:77-79` | — | Loopback-gated; consistency / sort. | TODO |
| S-039 | security | `target` accepted as any `typeof === 'number'`, including negative or absurdly large numbers (e.g. `1e308`). | `src/app/api/reading-goal/route.ts:37` | — | Loopback-gated; data quality. | TODO |
| S-040 | security | `q` parameter on `listUserActivity` flows into `LIKE ?` clauses without escaping `%`/`_`. A `q=%` matches every row. | `src/lib/activity.ts:137-141` | — | Loopback-gated. Lets a caller dump the entire activity log even when they only have substring auth-ed access. | TODO |
| S-041 | security | `JSON.parse(await file.text())` runs **after** size pre-check passes (good), but the parsed structure is then walked by `importData` which writes every accepted row into `collection`/`vn` tables. The schema validation is `Array.isArray(body.collection) && Array.isArray(body.vns)` only — individual rows can carry any shape. | `src/app/api/collection/import/route.ts:42` | — | Loopback-gated; data corruption / DoS. | TODO |
| S-042 | security | `importData` pushes `(e as Error).message` into `summary.errors[]`, which is returned to the client and recorded in `user_activity`. | `src/lib/db.ts:8379, 8415, 8431, 8441` | — | Loopback-gated; minor info disclosure. | TODO |
| S-043 | security | The "LIMIT 1" / "LIMIT ${safeLimit}" sanitizer drops `_` characters via `\\_` for Postgres LIKE-wildcard safety. The regex allow-list keeps `+`, `×`, etc. — fine — but the resulting query may include zero-width matches via the residual punctuation. The remote EGS DB has a 10_000 row cap; not a concern at our LIMIT 1/50. | `src/lib/erogamescape.ts:769-774, 808-813` | — | No active vulnerability. Documentation-grade. | TODO |
| S-044 | security | `vndbErrorResponse` matches `/401/.test(e.message)` to translate to a typed error. | SRC-API-001 | api | The `cleanup()` function sets `aborted = true` but the `cancel()` method (lines 74-76) can race with `req.signal.addEventListener('abort', cleanup)` (line 69). | SRC-API-004 | api | Routes validate VN IDs using `/^(v\d+\|egs_\d+)$/i` (case-insensitive flag). | SRC-API-006 | api | The `parseEgsId()` function (lines 29-35) strips `egs_` prefix, then converts to number. But a param like `egs_` (with nothing after underscore) becomes `""`, `Number("")` is 0, and the check `n <= 0` rejects it. However, a param like `egs_abc` becomes `Number("abc")` which is `NaN`, and `NaN <= 0` is `false`, so it's accepted as a valid ID. The route then calls `getEgsVnLink(egsId)` with `NaN`, which could cause unexpected behavior downstream. | `/api/egs/[id]/vndb/route.ts` lines 29-35 | — | - Use strict: `const n = Number(cleaned); if (!Number.isSafeInteger(n) \|\| n <= 0) return null;` | TODO |

I cleaned it into a deduplicated TODO backlog. I removed “good practice / no issue” entries and merged overlapping findings like focus indicators, search input labeling, provider job reuse, async pending states, and mobile table/overflow issues. Sources used: accessibility audit, API audit, stock/price audit, and UI/UX audit.    
I treated this one more aggressively: I removed rows that were clearly `FIXED_VERIFIED`, `ACCEPTED_RISK`, `Pass`, `Reference`, `None`, “Good”, “OK”, informational-only, or already marked as intentionally correct. I also merged repeated themes instead of blindly copying the same issue 5 times. The source file contains mixed i18n, performance/correctness, responsive, security, UX, accessibility, docs, QA, and round-checklist material.
